   function isIE () {
        var myNav = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
        return (myNav.indexOf("msie") != -1) ? parseInt(myNav.split("msie")[1]) : false;
      }
      function isChrome () {
        var myNavChrome = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
        return (myNavChrome.indexOf("chrome") != -1) ? parseInt(myNavChrome.split("chrome/")[1]) : false;
      }
      function isFirefox () {
        var myNavFirefox = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
        return (myNavFirefox.indexOf("firefox") != -1) ? parseInt(myNavFirefox.split("firefox/")[1]) : false;
      }

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var currenttime = 'June 22, 2018 21:29' //PHP method of getting server date
var serverdate= new Date(currenttime)

function padlength(zero) {
  var output=(zero.toString().length==1)? "0"+zero : zero
  return output
}
function displaytime() {
  serverdate.setSeconds(serverdate.getSeconds()+1)
  var timestring=padlength(serverdate.getHours())+":"+padlength(serverdate.getMinutes())
  document.getElementById("footerservertime").innerHTML=timestring
  if (document.getElementById("servertime")) {
  document.getElementById("servertime").innerHTML=timestring
  }
}

setInterval("displaytime()", 1000);
     </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var currenttime = "June 22, 2018 21:29:24"
               var serverdate= new Date(currenttime)

               function padlength(zero) {
                 var output=(zero.toString().length==1)? "0"+zero : zero
                 return output
               }
               function displaytime() {
                 serverdate.setSeconds(serverdate.getSeconds()+1)
                 var timestring = padlength(serverdate.getHours()) + ":" + padlength(serverdate.getMinutes())
                 document.getElementById("footerservertime").innerHTML=timestring
                 if (document.getElementById("servertime")) {
                   document.getElementById("servertime").innerHTML=timestring
                 }
               }
               setInterval("displaytime()", 1000);
     </script>
